<!-- External Script : Temp Button Disable -->
<script type="text/javascript">
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
    const selectors = [
        "body.so-con .rs-general-cta-section a.btn",
        "body.so-con .rs-so-con-page-hero-section a.btn"
    ];

    selectors.forEach(selector => {
        document.querySelectorAll(selector).forEach(el => {
            // Remove unwanted attributes
            ["data-toggle", "data-target", "aria-label"].forEach(attr => {
                el.removeAttribute(attr);
            });

            // Force links to open in a new tab
            el.setAttribute("target", "_blank");
            el.setAttribute("rel", "noopener noreferrer"); // security best practice
        });
    });
});
</script>
